webhook chain is implemented across multiple Go packages in the k8s.io/apiserver module, primarily within staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook. The implementation consists of three main components:\\n\\n## 1. Webhook Admission Controllers (Entry Points)\\n\\nTwo admission plugins implement the admission.Interface: MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook. Both are registered via the package init functions in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go respectively.\\n\\n- **MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): Implements the admission.MutationInterface. The Admit() method delegates to the generic Webhook.Dispatch() method. When a webhook patches the object, the mutatingDispatcher applies JSON patches and manages reinvocation of webhooks if the object changes.\\n\\n- **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): Implements the admission.ValidationInterface. The Validate() method also delegates to generic Webhook.Dispatch(). The validatingDispatcher calls webhooks in parallel and aggregates rejection responses.\\n\\n## 2. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nThe dispatch mechanism is implemented in the generic.Webhook type (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go). The Dispatch() method is the entry point that:\\n\\n1. Retrieves active webhooks from the hookSource (which is a configuration manager)\\n2. Calls the dispatcher's Dispatch() method with the admission attributes and webhooks\\n3. Returns early if the resource is exempt from webhooks (like webhook configuration resources themselves)\\n\\nEach plugin uses a specific dispatcher implementation:\\n\\n- **mutatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go): Sequentially calls mutating webhooks. For each webhook:\\n  1. Determines if the webhook should be called via ShouldCallHook() (rule matching, namespace/object selectors, match conditions)\\n  2. Creates AdmissionReview objects via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n  3. Calls the webhook via callAttrMutatingHook()\\n  4. Verifies the response via VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n  5. If the webhook returns a patch, applies it to the object using JSON Patch\\n  6. Tracks mutations in audit annotations\\n  7. Handles reinvocation when object changes\\n\\n- **validatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go): Calls validating webhooks in parallel. For each webhook:\\n  1. Determines if the webhook should be called via ShouldCallHook()\\n  2. Creates AdmissionReview objects via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n  3. Calls the webhook via callHook() in a goroutine\\n  4. Verifies the response via VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n  5. Collects errors in a channel and aggregates them\\n\\n## 3. Admission Response Aggregation\\n\\nBoth dispatchers use the shared VerifyAdmissionResponse() function (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go) to validate and extract information from AdmissionReview responses. This function:\\n\\n- Validates the response UID matches the request UID\\n- For mutating webhooks: ensures patch and patchType are both present or both absent\\n- For validating webhooks: ensures no patch or patchType is returned\\n- Returns an AdmissionResponse struct containing allowed status, patch, audit annotations, and warnings\\n\\nFor validating webhooks, responses are aggregated in the Dispatch() method of validatingDispatcher:\\n- Errors are collected in an error channel\\n- When all webhooks complete (via sync.WaitGroup), errors are aggregated\\n- If multiple rejections occur, all are logged but only the first is returned\\n- If any webhook rejects with FailurePolicy=Fail, the entire request is rejected\\n- If a webhook fails with FailurePolicy=Ignore, execution continues\\n\\nFor mutating webhooks, responses are handled sequentially:\\n- Each webhook's patch is immediately applied to the object\\n- Audit annotations and warnings are accumulated\\n- If a webhook rejects with FailurePolicy=Fail, request fails immediately\\n- If a webhook fails with FailurePolicy=Ignore, execution continues\\n- Patch annotations track what each webhook modified\\n\\n## 4. Configuration Management\\n\\nWebhook configurations are managed by configuration managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/):\\n\\n- **mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (mutating_webhook_manager.go): Watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration resources and provides the list of active webhooks via the Source interface\\n- **validatingWebhookConfigurationManager** (validating_webhook_manager.go): Watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration resources and provides the list of active webhooks\\n\\nBoth managers implement the generic.Source interface, allowing the generic webhook infrastructure to dynamically retrieve updated configurations.\\n\\n## 5. Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n- **WebhookAccessor** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go): Provides a unified interface to both MutatingWebhook and ValidatingWebhook objects, abstracting their differences\\n- **Error types** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/error.go): ErrCallingWebhook represents transport-layer errors, while ErrWebhookRejection represents explicit webhook rejections\\n- **WebhookInvocation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/interfaces.go): Tracks which webhook should be invoked with what resource/kind information\\n\\nThe webhook admission chain ensures that external webhooks can participate in the Kubernetes admission process by intercepting API requests, validating or mutating them, and returning decisions that are aggregated before the final admission verdict is made.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3319,"cache_read_input_tokens":92404,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3319},"output_tokens":4,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"bea8d9b1-a101-48ad-818e-32b69a0365b8","uuid":"ea424934-702b-4b5b-a16b-5ac03478a523"}

The implementation consists of three main components:\\n\\n## 1. Webhook Admission Controllers (Entry Points)\\n\\nTwo admission plugins implement the admission.Interface: MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook. Both are registered via the package init functions in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go respectively.\\n\\n- **MutatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go): Implements the admission.MutationInterface. The Admit() method delegates to the generic Webhook.Dispatch() method. When a webhook patches the object, the mutatingDispatcher applies JSON patches and manages reinvocation of webhooks if the object changes.\\n\\n- **ValidatingAdmissionWebhook** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go): Implements the admission.ValidationInterface. The Validate() method also delegates to generic Webhook.Dispatch(). The validatingDispatcher calls webhooks in parallel and aggregates rejection responses.\\n\\n## 2. Webhook Call Dispatch\\n\\nThe dispatch mechanism is implemented in the generic.Webhook type (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go). The Dispatch() method is the entry point that:\\n\\n1. Retrieves active webhooks from the hookSource (which is a configuration manager)\\n2. Calls the dispatcher's Dispatch() method with the admission attributes and webhooks\\n3. Returns early if the resource is exempt from webhooks (like webhook configuration resources themselves)\\n\\nEach plugin uses a specific dispatcher implementation:\\n\\n- **mutatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go): Sequentially calls mutating webhooks. For each webhook:\\n  1. Determines if the webhook should be called via ShouldCallHook() (rule matching, namespace/object selectors, match conditions)\\n  2. Creates AdmissionReview objects via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n  3. Calls the webhook via callAttrMutatingHook()\\n  4. Verifies the response via VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n  5. If the webhook returns a patch, applies it to the object using JSON Patch\\n  6. Tracks mutations in audit annotations\\n  7. Handles reinvocation when object changes\\n\\n- **validatingDispatcher** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go): Calls validating webhooks in parallel. For each webhook:\\n  1. Determines if the webhook should be called via ShouldCallHook()\\n  2. Creates AdmissionReview objects via CreateAdmissionObjects()\\n  3. Calls the webhook via callHook() in a goroutine\\n  4. Verifies the response via VerifyAdmissionResponse()\\n  5. Collects errors in a channel and aggregates them\\n\\n## 3. Admission Response Aggregation\\n\\nBoth dispatchers use the shared VerifyAdmissionResponse() function (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go) to validate and extract information from AdmissionReview responses. This function:\\n\\n- Validates the response UID matches the request UID\\n- For mutating webhooks: ensures patch and patchType are both present or both absent\\n- For validating webhooks: ensures no patch or patchType is returned\\n- Returns an AdmissionResponse struct containing allowed status, patch, audit annotations, and warnings\\n\\nFor validating webhooks, responses are aggregated in the Dispatch() method of validatingDispatcher:\\n- Errors are collected in an error channel\\n- When all webhooks complete (via sync.WaitGroup), errors are aggregated\\n- If multiple rejections occur, all are logged but only the first is returned\\n- If any webhook rejects with FailurePolicy=Fail, the entire request is rejected\\n- If a webhook fails with FailurePolicy=Ignore, execution continues\\n\\nFor mutating webhooks, responses are handled sequentially:\\n- Each webhook's patch is immediately applied to the object\\n- Audit annotations and warnings are accumulated\\n- If a webhook rejects with FailurePolicy=Fail, request fails immediately\\n- If a webhook fails with FailurePolicy=Ignore, execution continues\\n- Patch annotations track what each webhook modified\\n\\n## 4.
